class="p1">Attorney Advertising Disclosure</h3><p class="p1">Some law firm listings on this page are paid advertisements. Compensation may affect where and how law firms appear, including order of appearance.</p><h3 class="p1">How Law Firms Appear</h3><p class="p1">“Top-rated” and “Top” refer to law firms with strong publicly available consumer ratings and feedback, including information from third-party sources and reviews submitted on the Elite Litigators platform, and as determined by Elite Litigators’ proprietary methodology.</p><p class="p1">Law firms labeled as “Featured” or with the Featured Gavel icon are paid advertisements or paid placements. Law firms labeled as “Verified” participate in Elite Litigators’ Verified Program, which is an attorney advertising program and may include compensation for advertising or enhanced placement.</p><p class="p1">Inclusion, labeling, placement, or participation in any Elite Litigators program does not constitute and does not imply an endorsement, recommendation, guarantee of results, or that the quality of legal services provided by any law firm is greater than that of other lawyers or law firms.</p><p>Displayed numerical scores are proprietary ratings calculated by Elite Litigators. These ratings are based on aggregate consumer feedback, including data pulled from public review platforms and third-party sources, client reviews submitted directly to our platform, professional milestones including factors such as a firm’s experience, case results and standing within the legal community, and qualitative factors evaluated under our proprietary methodology. Ratings do not guarantee a specific outcome for your case, nor do they imply that a firm’s services are superior to those of others with different ratings.</p><p class="p1">Elite Litigators’ ratings are calculated on a state specific basis. A law firm’s numerical score in one state may differ from its score in another state. With the exception of Southern California and Upstate New York, which are treated as distinct rating jurisdictions and evaluated independently, ratings are calculated at a state level. Ratings within a state are comparative to and influenced by other law firms evaluated within that same state. Ratings are not calculated at a city or regional level. For firms operating in multiple cities or regions within the same state, data is aggregated and evaluated at the state level.</p><p class="p1">Elite Litigators assigns ratings only to law firms participating in its Verified Program. Law firms that are not verified may appear on the platform but are not rated.</p><h3 class="p1">Important Legal Information</h3><p class="p1">The information provided on this site is for general informational purposes only and does not constitute legal advice. Elite Litigators does not operate a lawyer referral service.</p><p class="p1">Attorneys listed in specific practice area sections are not certified as specialists or experts in any legal practice area unless specifically stated and certified by an ABA-accredited organization authorized by their jurisdiction.</p><p class="p1">No case outcomes are guaranteed. Based in Phoenix,<span class='dotted'>...</span> <span class='hide-text'>the firm focuses on injury-related claims arising from serious incidents that result in physical harm or loss.
The firm’s practice is built around guiding clients through the legal process after life-altering injuries, with an emphasis on clarity, responsiveness, and practical legal support from intake through resolution.
Working With the Firm  Injury-related legal matters often come at difficult moments. Phillips Law Group works with clients during these periods by helping them understand the legal process, their available options, and how a claim may move forward over time.
The firm emphasizes communication and consistency throughout a case, aiming to keep clients informed while managing the legal steps involved in pursuing a personal injury claim.
Practice Focus and Experience
Phillips Law Group’s practice reflects a focused approach to personal injury representation, shaped by the firm’s experience handling complex injury-related matters across Arizona.  A focus on serious injury and wrongful death matters that often involve long-term medical and personal consequences  Experience handling claims that require detailed investigation, coordination with medical documentation, and liability analysis  Representation in matters involving both individual defendants and commercial or institutional parties  A practice structured to support negotiation, litigation preparation, and case resolution within Arizona courts  Considering Next Steps
For individuals facing the aftermath of a serious injury or loss, having legal guidance can provide direction during a challenging time.  fill="#133C89"/> </g> <defs> <clipPath id="clip0_2392_927"> <rect width="107" height="88" fill="white"/> </clipPath> </defs> </svg></div><div class="content_area location-archive-posts__post_item_desc"> Morgan &amp; Morgan is a national personal injury law firm representing individuals harmed by negligence in motor vehicle accidents, premises liability<span class='dotted'>...</span> <span class='hide-text'>incidents, product-related injuries, and other serious injury matters. Founded in 1988, the firm has grown into one of the largest plaintiff-focused injury practices in the United States, with offices across multiple states and a practice centered on pursuing compensation for injured individuals and families.
Morgan &amp; Morgan is widely known for its contingency fee model and its long-standing focus on representing individuals against insurance companies, corporations, and other well-resourced defendants. The firm handles cases that range from more straightforward injury claims to complex disputes involving significant damages, contested liability, or prolonged litigation. This allows the legal teams to pursue matters that require both persistence and the ability to commit substantial legal resources over time.
Injury-Focused Representation at Scale
Morgan &amp; Morgan’s practice is built almost entirely around personal injury law. Rather than operating as a general-practice firm, its attorneys concentrate on injury-related claims, developing experience across recurring accident types and liability scenarios. This focus supports a consistent approach to investigating claims, valuing damages, and responding to defense strategies commonly used by insurers and corporate defendants.
Cases are handled with an eye toward preparation from the outset. Even when a matter is resolved through settlement, the firm’s approach emphasizes building the claim as though litigation may be required—gathering records, consulting experts when appropriate, and documenting damages in a way that supports full case value rather than quick resolution.
Case Handling and Client Access  Morgan &amp; Morgan promotes accessibility as a core part of its practice model. Clients typically engage with a legal team that manages communications with insurance carriers, coordinates documentation, and tracks procedural deadlines as a case moves forward. This structure is intended to reduce the administrative burden on injured individuals while keeping their claims active and moving toward resolution.
In many injury matters, clients can expect support that includes:  Direct handling of insurance communications and settlement negotiations  Collection and organization of records needed to document damages  Case development geared toward resolution through settlement or litigation, depending on how the matter progresses  Contingency-fee representation in many cases, meaning attorney fees are generally tied to recovery rather than paid upfront  Representing Injury Clients Across the United States
With offices across the country, Morgan &amp; Morgan handles personal injury claims in multiple jurisdictions while keeping its practice centered on injury law. The firm’s national reach can be a strong fit for clients who value broad coverage and the ability to pursue a claim with a team that routinely works across state lines.</span><a href="#" The firm handles injury-related claims arising from accidents, unsafe conditions, and other negligence-based matters.
The firm has represented thousands of clients in personal injury and related claims, including matters involving significant injuries, disputed liability, and insurance-related disputes that can develop after serious incidents.
Founded by attorney Larry Disparti, the practice has developed a public-facing identity centered on assertive injury representation and direct engagement with insurance carriers. The firm’s casework reflects a focus on helping injured individuals pursue recovery while managing the legal and insurance pressures that often follow serious harm.
Legal Protection Where It Matters Most
Disparti Law Group’s practice focuses on injury and rights-based claims where the outcome can have lasting financial and personal impact. Areas of representation include:  Auto Accidents – serious collisions involving cars, trucks, pedestrians, and rideshare vehicles  Premises Liability – slip and fall, trip hazards, negligent maintenance, and unsafe property conditions  Dog Bite Injuries – physical and emotional trauma from dog attacks, including cases involving children  Workers’ Compensation – job-related injuries, denied benefits, and employer retaliation  Social Security Disability – legal help with initial claims and appeals  Employment Law – wrongful termination, discrimination, harassment, and wage violations  Class Actions – collective actions involving consumer harm or systemic misconduct  Why People Hire Disparti Law Group
Individuals facing injury-related legal issues often evaluate firms based on experience, structure, and the ability to manage complex claims. Factors commonly associated with Disparti Law Group include:  Reported High-Value Case OutcomesThe firm is often associated with high-value injury and employment-related outcomes, particularly in matters involving significant harm or contested disputes.  Representation Across Thousands of ClaimsThe firm’s history includes work across a large volume of injury cases, reflecting exposure to a wide range of fact patterns and legal issues.  Contingency Fee StructureMany personal injury matters are handled on a contingency fee basis, meaning attorney fees are typically tied to case resolution rather than upfront payment.  Integrated Injury-Focused PracticeIn addition to personal injury claims, the firm maintains experience in disability and employment law matters that often intersect with injury-related disputes.  Early Case Action and Ongoing CommunicationThe firm emphasizes prompt engagement with claims and structured communication as a case progresses.  The Disparti Standard  Disparti Law Group represents individuals dealing with serious injuries, financial uncertainty, and long-term recovery concerns following an accident or workplace incident. The firm’s case approach reflects an emphasis on preparation, responsiveness, and sustained involvement throughout the legal process.
Rather than focusing on quick resolutions, the firm’s practice is structured to address claims that may involve extended medical treatment, contested liability, or resistance from insurance carriers. Clients considering Disparti Law Group often do so when the outcome of a case carries meaningful personal and financial weight.</span><a href="#" class="button-more">Read More</a></div><div With<span class='dotted'>...</span> <span class='hide-text'>offices across multiple states, the firm represents individuals in injury-related matters and is structured to handle claims under varying state-specific rules, procedures, and timelines.
The practice is structured to handle cases from early intake through resolution, including matters that require negotiation, detailed documentation, or litigation when a dispute cannot be resolved outside of court.
Practice Focus
The firm’s practice centers on personal injury representation, with work spanning a variety of accident and negligence-related claims. This includes motor vehicle accident cases involving cars, trucks, pedestrians, and rideshare vehicles, as well as matters where injuries result in long-term medical care or significant financial impact.
In addition, the firm represents clients in wrongful death claims and other injury-related disputes that often involve contested liability, insurance coverage questions, or more substantial damages issues. The practice is equipped to develop these matters through detailed medical documentation and structured case preparation, including litigation readiness when a dispute cannot be resolved through negotiation.
How the Firm Operates
Cases are handled through a coordinated team structure that can include attorneys, case managers, and support staff working together on the same matter. This approach is built to support:  Structured case development and documentation  Consistent communication and case updates  Litigation-ready preparation when a claim becomes contested  For individuals weighing their options after an injury, Alexander Shunnarah Trial Attorneys may be a strong fit for those who value an organized process, steady support throughout the claim, and a team transform="translate(0.00390625)"/> </clipPath> </defs> </svg> 866-549-2161 </a> <a target=""
 class="morgan-advertisement__button_consultation" href="https://elitelitigators.com/law-firm-reviews/morgan-morgan/free-consultation"> Free Consultation </a></div></div></aside></div></div></section><section class="content-text content-first "><div class="container content-text__wrapper"><div class="content_inner sidebar_content"><div class="content_white_list content_area"><h4><strong>Class Action Lawyers</strong></h4><p>Class action attorneys play a pivotal role in representing groups of people who have suffered similar injuries or damages from the actions of a corporation or entity. These legal professionals specialize in navigating the complex landscape of class action lawsuits, where they must prove that the issues affecting the class members are common enough to warrant a collective action. Their expertise not only lies in gathering and presenting evidence but also in negotiating settlements that fairly compensate the entire class. For example, class action lawsuits like the Equifax Data Breach Settlement and the Volkswagen Emissions Scandal illustrate their crucial role in addressing widespread consumer issues.</p><p>Understanding the distinction between class action and mass tort cases is crucial when seeking legal representation. In class action lawsuits, a group of plaintiffs is treated as a single entity, allowing for a unified trial that addresses common grievances against a defendant. This contrasts with mass torts, where each plaintiff may experience different injuries and may receive varying levels of compensation. Cases such as the <a href="https://elitelitigators.com/roundup/">Roundup Weed Killer Cancer Claims</a> and the <a href="https://elitelitigators.com/johnsons-talcum-powder/">Johnson’s Talcum Powder Lawsuit</a> are prime examples of mass torts where individual circumstances dictate the outcomes. Class action attorneys near you are adept at managing these dynamics, ensuring that all members of the class are adequately represented and receive compensation in line with the group’s collective experience.</p><p>In addition to class action cases, several significant mass torts have gained attention due to the widespread harm they have caused. For instance, the <a href="https://elitelitigators.com/hernia-mesh/">Hernia Mesh Implant Complications</a> involve individuals who have suffered severe injuries from defective surgical implants, while the <a href="https://elitelitigators.com/paraquat-lawsuit/">Paraquat Claims</a> address the devastating effects of this herbicide, which has been linked to Parkinson&#8217;s disease. Similarly, the <a href="https://elitelitigators.com/chemical-hair-relaxers/">Chemical Hair Relaxer Cancer Lawsuit</a> has emerged as a critical case, with plaintiffs claiming that long-term use of these products has led to serious health issues, including cancer. The <a href="https://elitelitigators.com/pfas-forever-chemicals/">PFAS Contamination Lawsuits</a> focus on the widespread contamination of water supplies by &#8220;forever chemicals&#8221; and the resulting health risks, impacting numerous communities. Additionally, the <a href="https://elitelitigators.com/paragard-lawsuit/">Paragard IUD Injury Claims</a> concern women who have experienced serious injuries from this birth control device, and the <a href="https://elitelitigators.com/firefighting-foam-lawsuit/">Firefighting Foam Cancer Lawsuit</a> involves firefighters and others exposed to toxic chemicals leading to cancer and other illnesses. For those affected by diabetes or weight loss medications, seeking help from a<a href="https://elitelitigators.com/drug-lawsuits/"> weight loss and diabetes drug lawsuit law firm</a> can ensure they receive expert guidance and support. Lastly, the <a href="https://elitelitigators.com/nec-infant-formula-lawsuit/">NEC Baby Formula Lawsuit</a> addresses the risks posed by certain infant formulas that have been linked to a potentially fatal condition in premature babies. Each of these mass torts highlights the importance of specialized legal representation to ensure victims receive the justice and compensation they deserve.</p><p>When searching for the right legal representation, Class Actions Attorney reviews can be an invaluable resource. These reviews shed light on the effectiveness and reliability of attorneys in handling complex class action lawsuits. Clients and legal professionals alike contribute insights, offering perspectives on case management, client communication, and overall success rates. Checking these reviews can help you make a well-informed decision when selecting a class action law firm. Ready to find your legal advocate? Explore our comprehensive list of class action attorneys today.</p></div><div class="content_faqs"><h3 class="notitle"> Answers to Commonly Asked Questions About Hiring a Class Actions Lawyer Near You</h3><div class="content_faqs--item"><div class="content_faqs--title"> <svg width="20" height="12" viewBox="0 0 20 12" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"> <path d="M2 2L10 10L18 2" stroke="#1D4CA5" stroke-width="3" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"/> </svg><h4>What is a class action attorney?</h4></div><div class="content_faqs--content">A class action attorney is a legal professional who represents a group of individuals collectively, known as a class, in a lawsuit against a defendant. These cases typically arise when a large number of people have been similarly harmed by the same defendant&#039;s actions.</div></div><div class="content_faqs--item"><div class="content_faqs--title"> <svg width="20" height="12" viewBox="0 0 20 12" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"> <path d="M2 2L10 10L18 2" stroke="#1D4CA5" stroke-width="3" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"/> </svg><h4>When should I contact a class action attorney?</h4></div><div class="content_faqs--content">You should contact a class action attorney near you if you and a group of people have suffered similar harm or damages due to the actions or negligence of a company or individual. This could include situations like defective products, false advertising, unfair business practices, or discrimination.</div></div><div class="content_faqs--item"><div class="content_faqs--title"> <svg width="20" height="12" viewBox="0 0 20 12" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"> <path d="M2 2L10 10L18 2" stroke="#1D4CA5" stroke-width="3" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"/> </svg><h4>How can a class action attorney help me?</h4></div><div class="content_faqs--content">A class action attorney near you can help you by evaluating your case, determining if a class action suit is appropriate, identifying other potential class members, filing the lawsuit on behalf of the class, and negotiating settlements or representing the class in court.</div></div><div class="content_faqs--item"><div class="content_faqs--title"> <svg width="20" height="12" viewBox="0 0 20 12" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"> <path d="M2 2L10 10L18 2" stroke="#1D4CA5" stroke-width="3" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"/> </svg><h4>What are the typical fees for a class action attorney?</h4></div><div class="content_faqs--content">Most class action attorneys work on a contingency fee basis, meaning they only get paid if they win your case. The fee is typically a percentage of the compensation the class receives, which can vary depending on the complexity of the case and the attorney&#039;s experience.</div></div><div class="content_faqs--item"><div class="content_faqs--title"> <svg width="20" height="12" viewBox="0 0 20 12" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"> <path d="M2 2L10 10L18 2" stroke="#1D4CA5" stroke-width="3" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"/> </svg><h4>What factors influence the outcome of a class action lawsuit?</h4></div><div class="content_faqs--content">Factors that can influence the outcome of a class action lawsuit include the number of individuals in the class, the severity of the harm done, the strength of the evidence, the financial resources of the defendant, and the skill and experience of the attorney.</div></div><div class="content_faqs--item"><div class="content_faqs--title"> <svg width="20" height="12" viewBox="0 0 20 12" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"> <path d="M2 2L10 10L18 2" stroke="#1D4CA5" stroke-width="3" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"/> </svg><h4>What is the process for starting a class action lawsuit?</h4></div><div class="content_faqs--content">Starting a class action lawsuit typically involves identifying the class of individuals who have been harmed, filing a complaint in court, and then seeking class certification from the court. The court will then decide whether the case can proceed as a class action.</div></div><div class="content_faqs--item"><div class="content_faqs--title"> <svg width="20" height="12" viewBox="0 0 20 12" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"> <path d="M2 2L10 10L18 2" stroke="#1D4CA5" stroke-width="3" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"/> </svg><h4>How long does it take to resolve a class action lawsuit?</h4></div><div class="content_faqs--content">The length of a class action lawsuit can vary widely, depending on the complexity of the case, the number of class members, the nature of the claims, and the court&#039;s schedule. It can take anywhere from a few months to several years.</div></div><div class="content_faqs--item"><div class="content_faqs--title"> <svg width="20" height="12" viewBox="0 0 20 12" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"> <path d="M2 2L10 10L18 2" stroke="#1D4CA5" stroke-width="3" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"/> </svg><h4>Can I opt out of a class action lawsuit?</h4></div><div class="content_faqs--content">Yes, if you are part of a class in a class action lawsuit, you generally have the right to opt out or exclude yourself from the class. If you opt out, you retain the right to file your own individual lawsuit, but you won&#039;t share in any settlement or judgment obtained in the class action.</div></div><div class="content_faqs--item"><div class="content_faqs--title"> <svg width="20" height="12" viewBox="0 0 20 12" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"> <path d="M2 2L10 10L18 2" stroke="#1D4CA5" stroke-width="3" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"/> </svg><h4>What is the difference between a class action and a mass tort?</h4></div><div class="content_faqs--content">While both class actions and mass torts involve large groups of plaintiffs, in a class action, the plaintiffs are treated as a single entity, whereas in a mass tort, each plaintiff is treated as an individual and can receive different amounts of compensation based on their individual circumstances.</div></div><div class="content_faqs--item"><div class="content_faqs--title"> <svg width="20" height="12" viewBox="0 0 20 12" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"> <path d="M2 2L10 10L18 2" stroke="#1D4CA5" stroke-width="3" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"/> </svg><h4>What types of cases are commonly handled by class action attorneys?</h4></div><div class="content_faqs--content">Class action attorneys commonly handle cases involving consumer fraud, defective products, securities fraud, antitrust violations, employment discrimination, and environmental harm, among others.</div></div> <script type="application/ld+json">{"@context":"https:\/\/schema.org","@type":"FAQPage","mainEntity":[{"@type":"Question","name":"What is a class action attorney?","acceptedAnswer":{"@type":"Answer","text":"A class action attorney is a legal professional who represents a group of individuals collectively, known as a class, in a lawsuit against a defendant. <script type="text/javascript">document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
                // Function to show the modal window
                function showJohnsonLawModal(message) {
                    var modal = document.getElementById('johnsonLawModal');
                    var messageElement = modal.querySelector('.johnson-law-modal-message');
                    messageElement.textContent = message;
                    modal.style.display = 'block';
                }

                // Closing the modal window
                var modal = document.getElementById('johnsonLawModal');
                var closeBtn = modal.querySelector('.johnson-law-modal-close');
                var okButton = modal.querySelector('.johnson-law-modal-button');

                function closeModal() {
                    modal.style.display = 'none';
                }

                closeBtn.onclick = closeModal;
                okButton.onclick = closeModal;
                window.onclick = function(event) {
                    if (event.target == modal) {
                        closeModal();
                    }
                }

                // Function to reset the value of Selectize
                function resetSelectizeValue(selectizeInstance) {
                    if (selectizeInstance) {
                        selectizeInstance.clear(true);
                    }
                }

                // Handlers for the form fields
                var forms = document.querySelectorAll('.wpcf7-form');

                forms.forEach(function(form) {
                    // Check if the hidden field law_firm_id with the correct values exists
                    var lawFirmIdField = form.querySelector('input[name="law_firm_id"][value="176371"], input[name="law_firm_id"][value="1276707"]');
                    var lawNameField = form.querySelector('input[name="law_name"][value="No Bull Law"]');
                    
                    if (!lawFirmIdField && !lawNameField) {
                        return;
                    }

                    // Function to initialize the selects
                    function initializeSelectize() {
                        var selects = form.querySelectorAll('select.wpcf7-form-control');
                        selects.forEach(function(select) {
                            // Check if the select is not already initialized
                            if (!select.classList.contains('selectized') && !select.selectize) {
                                try {
                                    $(select).selectize({
                                        onInitialize: function() {
                                            var selectize = this;
                                            var selectName = select.name;
                                            
                                            // Configure handlers for specific selects
                                            if (selectName === 'attorney_select-123' || 
                                                selectName === 'fault_select-123') {
                                                selectize.on('change', function(value) {
                                                    if (value === 'Yes') {
                                                        showJohnsonLawModal('We are sorry, this law firm is only taking clients who answered No to this question.');
                                                        setTimeout(() => resetSelectizeValue(this), 0);
                                                    }
                                                });
                                            } else if (selectName === 'injured_select-123' ||
                                                      selectName === 'otherfield6' ||
                                                      selectName === 'otherfield10') {
                                                selectize.on('change', function(value) {
                                                    if (value === 'No') {
                                                        showJohnsonLawModal('We are sorry, this law firm is only taking clients who answered Yes to this question.');
                                                        setTimeout(() => resetSelectizeValue(this), 0);
                                                    }
                                                });
                                            }
                                        }
                                    });
                                    console.log('Initialized selectize for', select.name);
                                } catch (e) {
                                    console.error('Error initializing selectize:', e);
                                }
                            }
                        });
                    }

                    // Initialize the selects when the page is loaded and with a small delay
                    // to ensure the full loading of the DOM
                    initializeSelectize();
                    setTimeout(initializeSelectize, 500);
                    setTimeout(initializeSelectize, 1000);

                    // Observe the dynamic changes of the form
                    var observer = new MutationObserver(function(mutations) {
                        // Call the initialization with a delay
                        setTimeout(initializeSelectize, 100);
                    });

                    observer.observe(form, {
                        childList: true,
                        subtree: true
                    });
                });
            });</script> <script defer src="https://elitelitigators.com/wp-includes/js/dist/hooks.min.js?ver=4d63a3d491d11ffd8ac6" id="wp-hooks-js"></script> <script defer
